country_event = {
	id = bormann.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.0" }
	title = bormann.0.t
	desc = bormann.0.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_street

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = bormann.0.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = bormann.0.a_tt
		hidden_effect = { BOR_Influence_Initialize = yes }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = bormann.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = WORLD.2056 }
		}		
	}
}

country_event = { #anti heydrich pact from speer
	id = bormann.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.8"}
    title = bormann.8.t
    desc = bormann.8.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_Army

	trigger = {
		country_exists = HGR
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = bormann.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GGR }
			GGR = { country_event = goering.8 } #continue
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				anti_heydrich_pact_script = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bormann.8.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GGR }
			GGR = { country_event = goering.8 } #continue
			SGR = { country_event = speer.19 } #rejected by bormann
		}
		else = {
			SGR = { country_event = speer.17 } #dead in water
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Encroach on Speidel's Germania
	id = bormann.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.12"}
    title = bormann.12.t
    desc = bormann.12.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_Army

    fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = bormann.12.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.1
		transfer_state = 776
		transfer_state = 1026
		hidden_effect = {
		    country_event = {
	            id = bormann.13
		        days = 31
	        }
		}
    }
	
    option = {
        name = bormann.12.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = HGR
			HGR = {
				OR = {
					controls_state = 68
					controls_state = 59
					controls_state = 60
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		hidden_effect = {
		    HGR = {
		        country_event = {
			        id = HGR.15
				    days = 3
			    }
		    }
		}
    }
	
	option = {
        name = bormann.12.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = SGR
			SGR = {
				OR = {
					controls_state = 60
					controls_state = 59
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		hidden_effect = {
		    SGR = {
		        country_event = {
			        id = speer.22
				    days = 3
			    }
		    }
		}
    }
	
	option = {
        name = bormann.12.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {				
					HGR = {
						controls_state = 68
						controls_state = 59
						controls_state = 60				 
					}
			}
			NOT = {
					SGR = {
						controls_state = 60
						controls_state = 59
					}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		hidden_effect = {
		    GGR = {
		        country_event = {
			        id = goering.6
				    days = 31
			    }
			}
		}
    }
}

country_event = { # Continue to encroach on Speidel's Germania
	id = bormann.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.13"}
    title = bormann.13.t
    desc = bormann.13.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_Army

    fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = bormann.13.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		declare_war_on = {
            target = GER
            type = annex_everything
        }
		hidden_effect = {
		    GGR = { country_event = { id = goering.40 days = 1 } }
			HGR = { country_event = { id = HGR.20 days = 1 } }
			SGR = { country_event = { id = speer.26 days = 1 } }
			set_global_flag = GER_Scramble_For_Germania
		}
    }
	
    option = {
        name = bormann.13.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.1
		transfer_state = 1025
		hidden_effect = {
		    country_event = {
	            id = bormann.14
		        days = 25
	        }
		}
    }
	
	option = {
        name = bormann.13.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		hidden_effect = {
		    country_event = {
	            id = bormann.13
		        days = 31
	        }
		}
    }
}

#The Question of Slavery
country_event = {
	id = bormann.26
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.26" }
	title = bormann.26.t
	desc = bormann.26.desc
	picture = GFX_report_generic_prisoners2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Build ghettos in the cities
		name = bormann.26.a
		BOR_SIG_SP_10_2 = yes		
		BOR_SIG_SL_10_2_2 = yes		
		BOR_SIG_AP_2_2 = yes		
		BOR_SIG_AL_2_2_1 = yes		
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
	option = { # Restore the slave camps
		name = bormann.26.b
		BOR_SIG_AP_10_2 = yes		
		BOR_SIG_AL_10_2_1 = yes		
		BOR_SIG_SP_2_2 = yes		
		BOR_SIG_SL_2_2_0 = yes		
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

# A Meeting with the Wehrmacht's Leaders
country_event = {
	id = bormann.28
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.28" }
	title = bormann.28.t
	desc = bormann.28.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Let's hear them out
		name = bormann.28.a
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.29
			days = 1
		}
		set_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 0 }
		set_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 0 }
	}
}

# Speidel VS. Schörner, ROUND 1: FIGHT! - The Future Direction
country_event = {
	id = bormann.29
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.29" }
	title = bormann.29.t
	desc = bormann.29.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # We must adapt our strategies to this new age of warfare.
		name = bormann.29.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_speidel
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.30
			days = 1
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = land_doctrine
		}
		add_to_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 1 }
	}
	option = { # Our strategies won us the war, there's no need to change them.
		name = bormann.29.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_schorner
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.30
			days = 1
		}
		add_war_support = 0.075
		add_to_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 1 }
	}
}

# Speidel VS. Schörner, ROUND 2: FIGHT! - Conscription
country_event = {
	id = bormann.30
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.30" }
	title = bormann.30.t
	desc = bormann.30.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # A smaller and professional army is ideal.
		name = bormann.30.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_speidel
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.31
			days = 1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = tno_draft_exemptions_none
 			add_idea = tno_draft_exemptions_educational_deferment
		}
		add_to_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 1 }
	}
	option = { # All brave sons of Germany must fight.
		name = bormann.30.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_schorner
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.31
			days = 1
		}
		add_manpower = 50000
		add_to_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 1 }
	}
}

# Speidel VS. Schörner, FINAL ROUND: FIGHT! - The Role of the Wehrmacht
country_event = {
	id = bormann.31
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.31" }
	title = bormann.31.t
	desc = bormann.31.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Military interference in politics will lead to no good.
		name = bormann.31.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_speidel
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.32
			days = 1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = tno_military_supervision_kill_em_all
 			add_idea = tno_military_supervision_military_policing
		}
		add_to_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 1 }
	}
	option = { # The Wehrmacht should have a political role.
		name = bormann.31.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_schorner
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.32
			days = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_to_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 1 }
	}
}

# The Result
country_event = {
	id = bormann.32
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.32" }
	title = bormann.32.t
	desc = { text = bormann.32.desc_speidel_victory trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_speidel_point > bormann_schorner_point } } }
	desc = { text = bormann.32.desc_schorner_victory trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_schorner_point > bormann_speidel_point } } }
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Speidel wins
		name = bormann.32.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_speidel_point > bormann_schorner_point } }
		BOR_SIG_AS_0_15 = yes
		set_country_flag = BOR_speidel_okw
		clear_variable = bormann_speidel_point
		clear_variable = bormann_schorner_point
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = BOR_Dismantlement_I.100 days = 30 } }
	}
	option = { # Schörner wins oh god oh fuck
		name = bormann.32.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_schorner_point > bormann_speidel_point } }
		BOR_SIG_AS_2_15 = yes
		set_country_flag = BOR_schorner_okw
		clear_variable = bormann_speidel_point
		clear_variable = bormann_schorner_point
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = BOR_Dismantlement_I.1 days = 30 } }
	}
}

		name = bormann.1508.a
		if = {
			limit = { GGN = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } } }
			GGN = { save_party_popularities = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = GGN
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_reichskommissariat
				}
			}
			else = { puppet = GGN }
			GGN = { apply_party_popularities = yes }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = bormann.161 days = 7 } 
		}
	}
}

#The Polish response arrives in Germania, Warschau Telegram
country_event = {
    id = bormann.154
    immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.154" }
	title = bormann.154.t
    #Polish say yes
    desc = { text = bormann.154.desc_agreed trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_accepted_protection } }
    #Polish say no
    desc = { text = bormann.154.desc_declined trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_denied_submission } }
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_agreement
    fire_only_once = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    #Reichsprotektorat accepted
    option = {
        trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_accepted_protection }
		name = bormann.154.a_accepted
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = bormann.155 }
			GGN = { annex_country = { target = POL transfer_troops = no } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = GGN
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_reichskommissariat
				}
			}
			else = { puppet = GGN }
			GGN = {
				set_popularities = {
					national_socialism = 80
					fascism = 20
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = RPO_protectorate
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Albert Forster"
					desc = "POLITICS_ALBERT_FORSTER_DESC"

					expire = "1984.10.28"
					ideology = national_socialism_subtype
					traits = { terrorizer }
				}
			}
		}
    }

    #Polish say no
    option = {
        trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_denied_submission }
		name = bormann.154.a_declined
		BOR_SIG_SP_0_10 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = bormann.155 }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = GER_bormann_polish_humiliation  days = 180 }
			country_event = {id = bormann.157 days = 7 } 
		}
    }
}

			country = SWE

		SWE = { add_ideas = Pakt_Observer }
		hidden_effect = {country_event = {id = bormann.1647 days = 1}}
		add_stability = 0.1
	}

}

				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure  level = 1 instant_build = yes }
		}
		
		150 = {
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure  level = 2 instant_build = yes }
		}
		
		148 = {
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure  level = 4 instant_build = yes }
		}
		
		722 = {
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure  level = 3 instant_build = yes }
		}
			
		add_to_variable = {national_debt = 4000}
		add_to_variable = { fin_agree = 5 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_debt
		hidden_effect = {country_event = {id = bormann.1639 days = 3} }
	}
	
	#No
	option = {
		name = bormann.1638.b
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FIN
			modifier = GER_FIN_rejected_petsamo_road
		}
		add_to_variable = { fin_agree = -5 }
		hidden_effect = {country_event = {id = bormann.1639 days = 3} }
	}
}

    title = bormann.1647.t
	desc = { text = bormann.1647.d }
	
	picture = GFX_news_event_stockholm_treaty
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = GER}
		name = bormann.1647.a
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { tag = SWE }
		name = bormann.1647.b
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = SWE
			}
		}
		name = bormann.1647.c
	}
}

#Bormann attempts to enter RANDOM EUROPEAN RK (FIRE FOR RANDOM EUROPEAN RK)
country_event = {
	id = bormann.101
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.101"}
    title = bormann.101.t
    desc = bormann.101.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_Army
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Yea
		name = bormann.101.a
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = has_bormann }
		log = "[This.GetName] accepted Bormann"
		#Effects for country here
	}
	option = { #Nah
		name = bormann.101.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rejected_bormann
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = CZE
						original_tag = DEN
						original_tag = HOL
						original_tag = MCW
						original_tag = SLO
						original_tag = CZE
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = rejected_bormann }
				}
				country_event = { id = bormann.101 days = 3 random = 24 }
				ROOT = { set_temp_variable = { bormann_option = 1 } }
			}
			#Speer is dead if there's nobody else to flee to
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { bormann_option = 1 } } }
				set_global_flag = bormann_dead
				every_country = {
					news_event = { id = bormann.102 days = 3 random = 24 }
				}
				log = "[This.GetName] rejected Bormann, Bormann dead"
			}
		}
		log = "[This.GetName] rejected Bormann"
	}
}

		}
		else = { puppet = CZE }

		country_event = { id = bormann.601 days = 4 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Unleashing the Orpo
	id = bormann.652
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.652" }
	title = bormann.652.t
	desc = {
		text = bormann.652.desc.a # Geelkerken
		trigger = {
			HOL = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HOL_musserist_rk
					has_country_flag = HOL_fascist_independence
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Bieshuevel
	desc = { text = bormann.652.desc.b trigger = { HOL = { has_country_flag = HOL_biesheuvel_government } } }
	# Democracy
	desc = { text = bormann.652.desc.c trigger = { HOL = { has_country_flag = HOL_towards_democracy } } }
	# SS
	desc = { text = bormann.652.desc.d trigger = { HOL = { has_country_flag = HOL_SS_in_power } } }
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_arrest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = bormann.652.a
		BOR_SIG_AP_0_3 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AP_6_3 = yes
		HOL = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_SS_in_power }
				add_popularity = { ideology = burgundian_system 		popularity = -0.05 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = ultranational_socialism 	popularity = -0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = HOL_fascist_independence
						has_country_flag = HOL_musserist_rk
					}
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_biesheuvel_government }
				add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = -0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_towards_democracy }
				add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat 	popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative	 	popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal 			popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat 			popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = socialist 				popularity = -0.02 }
				
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_socialism popularity = 0.1 }
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_manpower = -2000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HOL = { has_country_flag = HOL_SS_in_power } }
			country_event = { id = bormann.682 days = 3 }
		}
		else =  { country_event = { id = bormann.653 days = 12 } }
	}
}

					name = "Franz Walter Stahlecker"

					OST_United_for_Ostland

					OST_Haste_Makes_Waste
					OST_Prussian_Values
				}
				load_focus_tree = OST_empty
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NORCoup_failure
			}
		}

country_event = { # Negotiations succeed
	id = bormann.1067
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1067"}
	title = bormann.1067.t
	desc = bormann.1067.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = bormann.1067.a
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					give_military_access = GER
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_1
			} 
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					give_military_access = GER
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = GER
						relation = docking_rights
						active = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = GER
						relation = docking_rights
						active = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_pakt_membership }
			add_to_faction = NOR
			hidden_effect = {
				NOR = {
					remove_faction_status = yes
					add_ideas = Pakt_Bundnispartner
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = NOR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			give_guarantee = NOR
			hidden_effect = {
				NOR = {
					remove_faction_status = yes
					add_ideas = Pakt_Observer
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_choose_kopenhagen
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_choose_oslo
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_choose_goteborg
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_garrison_rights
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_garrison_rights
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_economic_program
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_economic_program
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_pakt_membership
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_preparing_coup

		set_country_flag = BOR_NOR_negotiation_success
	}
	option = { #
		name = bormann.1067.a
		trigger = { tag = NOR }
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # 
		name = bormann.1105.a
		add_political_power = 40
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = UKR
				autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotektorat
			}
		}
		else = {
			puppet = UKR
			hidden_effect = { UKR = { set_cosmetic_tag = FUK_GER } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism }
				set_popularities = {
					social_conservative = 4
					authoritarian_democrat = 12
					despotism = 30
					fascism = 46
					national_socialism = 8
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = fascism
					name = "UKR_Bormann_fascism_party_name"
					long_name = "UKR_Bormann_fascism_party_name_long"
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Theodor Oberländer"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Theodor_Oberlander.dds"
					expire = "1999.4.24"
					ideology = fascism_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = UKR_collab
	}
}

			}

		clr_country_flag = BOR_Phase2
		set_country_flag = BOR_Phase3

}

country_event = { # UAR bounty time
	id = bormann.1213
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1213" }
	title = bormann.1213.t
	desc = bormann.1213.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_arab_soldiers1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # 
		name = bormann.1213.a
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_pp_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_war_support_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
		multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_pp_bonus = 3 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_war_support_bonus = 0.001 }
		add_political_power = BOR_OC_pp_bonus
		add_war_support = BOR_OC_war_support_bonus
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BOR_OC_participation > 30 } }
			set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
			set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
			multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 20 }
			divide_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 5000 }

			# Economic bonuses are proportional to the UAR's size
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 446 } } # Egypt
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 294 } } # Oman
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 293 } } # Yemen
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 291 } } # Iraq
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 656 } } # The Gulf
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 1306 } } # The Levant
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { money_reserves = BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus }
			add_to_variable = { GDP_growth = BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus }
			custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_money_reserves
			custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_GDP_growth
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BOR_OC_participation > 60 } }
			UAR = { add_ideas = GER_Bormann_OC_UAR_trade }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BOR_OC_participation > 80 } }
			UAR = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 291 } }
		}
		clear_variable = BOR_OC_participation
	}
}

						USA = { is_faction_leader = yes }
						ITA = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
					}
					add_ideas = OFN_Independent_Member
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
						ITA = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
					}
					add_ideas = Sphere_Coequal
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ITA = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					}
					add_ideas = TRI_Member_Client
				}
			}
			every_country = { news_event = { id = WORLD.664 days = 1 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}

		name = bormann.1717.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

country_event = { # Hidden event to choose a random RK if the player has not made a selection
	id = bor_econ.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bor_econ.1" }
	title = "Bormann Econ Selection Disabler"
	desc = "You shouldn't be seeing this"
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_flag = BOR_EconMech_RK_select }
	
	option = {
		name = "Ok"
		BOR_EconMech_RK_selection_complete = yes
	}
}

	id = bor_econ.100
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bor_econ.100" }
	title = bor_econ.100.t
	desc = bor_econ.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_germany_court
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = bor_econ.100.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Bormann needs to decide on a main megacorp to use in his plans, briefly explaining each corp and their advantages
	id = bor_econ.101
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bor_econ.101" }
	title = bor_econ.101.t
	desc = bor_econ.101.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_meeting_table
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = bor_econ.101.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_seimens_collatral
		add_to_variable = {
			var = misc_costs
			value = 50
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bor_econ.102
			days = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bor_econ.101.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_benz_collatral
		add_to_variable = {
			var = misc_costs
			value = 100
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bor_econ.103
			days = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bor_econ.101.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_reichswerke_collatral
		add_to_variable = {
			var = misc_costs
			value = 200
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bor_econ.104
			days = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bor_econ.101.d
		custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_farben_collatral
		add_to_variable = {
			var = misc_costs
			value = 300
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bor_econ.105
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Bormann meets with Siemens, lowest cost but lowest reward. Siemens is however the most loyal
	id = bor_econ.102
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bor_econ.102" }
	title = bor_econ.102.t
	desc = bor_econ.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungary_handshake
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = bor_econ.102.a
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_BOR_Econ_megacorp_help_seimens }
		set_variable = {
			var = BOR_Econ_ONE_GER_megacorp_political_power
			value = 0.2
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = BOR_Econ_ONE_GER_megacorp_construction_speed
			value = 0.02
		}
	}
}
